    var googletag_adunits_options = window.googletag_adunits_options || [];

    var googletag_adunits_isDisplayed = function(eElement) {
        try {
            var element = eElement.parentNode;
            return ("none" !== (element.currentStyle ? element.currentStyle.display : getComputedStyle(element, null).display));
        } catch (e) {
            return false;
        }
    }

    function googletag_push(sAdunit_slot, aAdunit_supported_sizes, sAdunit_div_id, oOptions) {
        _satellite.notify("DFP: AdUnit Rendering Starting ==================================================================", 3);
        // If any of the 3 first parameters missing, return false
        if (typeof sAdunit_slot != 'string' || !sAdunit_slot ||
            !googletag_isArr(aAdunit_supported_sizes) || !aAdunit_supported_sizes ||
            typeof sAdunit_div_id != 'string' || !sAdunit_div_id ||
            !googletag_adunits_isDisplayed(document.getElementById(sAdunit_div_id))) {
            _satellite.notify("DFP: AdUnit Not rendered. Div (" + sAdunit_div_id + ") isDisplayed: " + googletag_adunits_isDisplayed(document.getElementById(sAdunit_div_id)), 3);
            return false;
        }
        googletag_adunits_params.push({});
        var nLastAdunit = googletag_adunits_params.length - 1;
        googletag_adunits_params[nLastAdunit].sAdunit_slot = sAdunit_slot;
        googletag_adunits_params[nLastAdunit].aAdunit_supported_sizes = aAdunit_supported_sizes;
        googletag_adunits_params[nLastAdunit].sAdunit_div_id = sAdunit_div_id;
        googletag_adunits_params[nLastAdunit].oOptions = oOptions;

        googletag.cmd.push(function() {

            var oParams = window.googletag_adunits_params.shift(),
                googletag = window.googletag;

            var sAdunit_slot = oParams.sAdunit_slot;
            var aAdunit_supported_sizes = oParams.aAdunit_supported_sizes;
            var sAdunit_div_id = oParams.sAdunit_div_id;
            var oOptions = oParams.oOptions;

            /**
             * Create an array of paths so that we can target DFP ads to Page URI's
             * @return Array an array of URL parts that can be targeted.
             */
            var getUrlTargeting = function(url) {

                // Get the url and parse it to its component parts using regex from RFC2396 Appendix-B (https://tools.ietf.org/html/rfc2396#appendix-B)
                var urlMatches = (url || window.location.toString()).match(/^(([^:/?#]+):)?(\/\/([^/?#]*))?([^?#]*)(\?([^#]*))?(#(.*))?/);
                var matchedAuthority = urlMatches[4] || '';
                var matchedPath = (urlMatches[5] || '').replace(/(.)\/$/, '$1');
                var matchedQuery = urlMatches[7] || '';

                // Get the query params for targeting against
                var params = matchedQuery.replace(/\=/ig, ':').split('&');

                return {
                    Host: matchedAuthority,
                    Path: matchedPath,
                    Query: params
                };
            }
            // Check to see if a new DIV id must be generated in case of duplicate on the same page?
            // if (googletag_div_adunits.indexOf("") != -1) {
            // 		logic to suffix the div id and ... how to send it back to the insertion command in Target?
            // }


            var sUrl = window.location.toString().replace(/\b[A-Z0-9._%+-]+@[A-Z0-9.-]+\.[A-Z]{2,4}\b/gi, '');
            var oUrlTargeting = getUrlTargeting(sUrl);

            var oSizeMapping = googletag.sizeMapping()
                // Too small to show ad
                .addSize([0, 0], googletag_adunits_getSizes([0, 0], aAdunit_supported_sizes))
                // Mobile Portrait - xs
                .addSize([120, 0], googletag_adunits_getSizes([120, 0], aAdunit_supported_sizes))
                // Mobile Landscape / Tablet Portrait - sm
                .addSize([360, 0], googletag_adunits_getSizes([360, 0], aAdunit_supported_sizes))
                // Viewport [640, 0]
                .addSize([640, 0], googletag_adunits_getSizes([640, 0], aAdunit_supported_sizes))
                // Tablet Landscape - md
                .addSize([768, 0], googletag_adunits_getSizes([768, 0], aAdunit_supported_sizes))
                // Viewport [980, 0]
                .addSize([980, 0], googletag_adunits_getSizes([980, 0], aAdunit_supported_sizes))
                // Laptop - lg
                .addSize([1024, 0], googletag_adunits_getSizes([1024, 0], aAdunit_supported_sizes))
                // Desktop - xl
                .addSize([1280, 0], googletag_adunits_getSizes([1280, 0], aAdunit_supported_sizes))
                .build();

            // Set default options for Adunits
            oOptions_default = {
                sAdunit_slot: sAdunit_slot,
                aAdunit_supported_sizes: aAdunit_supported_sizes,
                sAdunit_div_id: sAdunit_div_id,
                enableSingleRequest: false,
                collapseEmptyDivs: true,
                sizeMapping: oSizeMapping,
                setTargeting: {
                    'UrlHost': oUrlTargeting.Host,
                    'UrlPath': oUrlTargeting.Path,
                    'UrlQuery': oUrlTargeting.Query,
                    'language': (window["icl_vars"] && window["icl_vars"]["current_language"] ? window["icl_vars"]["current_language"] : ""),
                    'section': [($("meta[property='article:section']").attr('content') || "")],
                    'keywords': ($('ul[itemprop^="keywords"]').text().trim().replace(/,/g, "").replace(/\n+/g, ',').replace(/\s+/g, ' ').replace(/\s,\s/g, ',') || "").split(",")
                }
            };
            if (typeof oOptions != 'object' || typeof oOptions == 'undefined')
                oOptions = {};

            // Merge default options
            googletag_adunits_options.push({});
            var nLastAdunit = googletag_adunits_options.length - 1;
            for (var attrname in oOptions_default) {
                if (!googletag_adunits_options[nLastAdunit][attrname] && (googletag_isArr(oOptions_default[attrname]) || (typeof oOptions_default[attrname] != 'object')))
                    googletag_adunits_options[nLastAdunit][attrname] = oOptions_default[attrname];
                else if (typeof oOptions_default[attrname] == 'object') {
                    for (var j in oOptions_default[attrname]) {
                        if (typeof googletag_adunits_options[nLastAdunit][attrname] == 'undefined' || typeof googletag_adunits_options[nLastAdunit][attrname][j] == 'undefined') {
                            googletag_adunits_options[nLastAdunit][attrname] = googletag_adunits_options[nLastAdunit][attrname] || {};
                            googletag_adunits_options[nLastAdunit][attrname][j] = oOptions_default[attrname][j];
                        }
                    }
                }
            }

            var oOptions = window.googletag_adunits_options.shift(),
                googletag = window.googletag;
            if (oOptions.aAdunit_supported_sizes[0] == "out of page") {
                var adSlot = googletag.defineOutOfPageSlot(oOptions.sAdunit_slot, oOptions.sAdunit_div_id);
                _satellite.notify("DFP: AdUnit defineOutOfPageSlot: Slot = " + oOptions.sAdunit_slot + "", 3);
                _satellite.notify("DFP: AdUnit defineOutOfPageSlot: Div ID = " + oOptions.sAdunit_div_id + "", 3);
            } else {
                var adSlot = googletag.defineSlot(oOptions.sAdunit_slot, oOptions.aAdunit_supported_sizes, oOptions.sAdunit_div_id);
                _satellite.notify("DFP: AdUnit defineSlot: Slot = " + oOptions.sAdunit_slot + "", 3);
                _satellite.notify("DFP: AdUnit defineSlot: Supported sizes = " + oOptions.aAdunit_supported_sizes + "", 3);
                _satellite.notify("DFP: AdUnit defineSlot: Div ID = " + oOptions.sAdunit_div_id + "", 3);
                if (oOptions.sizeMapping) adSlot.defineSizeMapping(oOptions.sizeMapping);
                _satellite.notify("DFP: AdUnit defineSizeMapping: " + oOptions.sizeMapping + "", 3);
            }

            if (oOptions.enableSingleRequest) {
                googletag.pubads().enableSingleRequest();
                _satellite.notify("DFP: AdUnit enableSingleRequest: " + oOptions.enableSingleRequest + "", 3);
            }
            if (oOptions.collapseEmptyDivs) {
                if (googletag_isArr()) {
                    adSlot.setCollapseEmptyDiv(oOptions.collapseEmptyDivs[0] || false, oOptions.collapseEmptyDivs[1] || false);
                    _satellite.notify("DFP: AdUnit setCollapseEmptyDiv: " + (oOptions.collapseEmptyDivs[0] || false) + (oOptions.collapseEmptyDivs[1] || false) + "", 3);
                } else {
                    adSlot.setCollapseEmptyDiv(oOptions.collapseEmptyDivs || false);
                    _satellite.notify("DFP: AdUnit setCollapseEmptyDiv: " + (oOptions.collapseEmptyDivs || false) + "", 3);
                }
            }
            if (oOptions.setTargeting) {
                for (var i in oOptions.setTargeting) {
                    adSlot.setTargeting(i, oOptions.setTargeting[i]);
                    _satellite.notify("DFP: AdUnit setTargeting (key/values): " + i + " = " + oOptions.setTargeting[i] + "", 3);
                }
            }
            adSlot.addService(googletag.pubads());
            googletag.enableServices();
            googletag.display(oOptions.sAdunit_div_id);
            _satellite.notify("DFP: AdUnit Rendering Ended ====================================================================", 3);
        });
    }

    // Check if is array type (compatible with older browsers)
    function googletag_isArr(data) {
        try {
            return Object.prototype.toString.call(data) == '[object Array]';
        } catch (e) {
            return false;
        }
    }

    function googletag_isItemInArray(array, item) {
        for (var i = 0; i < array.length; i++) {
            // This if statement depends on the format of your array
            if ((array[i][0] == item[0] && array[i][1] == item[1]) ||
                (array[i] == "fluid" && array[i] == item[0]))
                return true; // Found it
        }
        return false; // Not found
    }
</script>

  $(document).ready(function() {
    var destinationPage = "'https://www.nbc.ca/personal/accounts/be-a-client.html'";
    var specificClass = "DTM-cta:Personal:at0083-BecomeClient:Header-ContextLink";
    $(".bncr-header-secondary-navigation-logon").attr("onclick", "window.location.href = " + destinationPage + "").addClass(specificClass);

<script>

        (function(){

        var dataLayerViewEventName = '' || '';
        var dataLayerViewLayerProperties = [];
        var $el;

        

        if(dataLayerViewEventName.trim().length) {

        var obj = {
        dataLayerViewEventName: dataLayerViewEventName,
        componentId: "c0f8a2f3-f931-47c7-b683-08fdcd7caabe_parsys_panelcontainer_19435_parsys_panelcontainer_parsys_textandimage" ,
        dataLayerViewLayerProperties: dataLayerViewLayerProperties
        };

        // IE11 trick (because IE11 don't know document.currentScript):
        https://stackoverflow.com/questions/403967/how-may-i-reference-the-script-tag-that-loaded-the-currently-executing-script
        if(document.currentScript){
        $el = document.currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        } else {
        var scripts = document.getElementsByTagName( 'script' );
        var currentScript = scripts[scripts.length - 1];
        $el = currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        }

        $el.setAttribute('data-dataLayerViewEventJson', JSON.stringify(
        Websites.DataLayer.cleanViewEventJSON(obj)));
        $el.setAttribute("data-dataLayerViewEvent", 'true');

        Websites.DataLayer.updateDataLayerViewEventElementsArray();

        }

        })();

        </script>
</div>
<script>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*
		*/

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

		</script></div>
</div>
</div>

<script type="text/javascript">
		
			var Websites = Websites || {};
			Websites.FragmentPicture = Websites.FragmentPicture || {
				init: function(viewport) {
					Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(viewport);
				},
	
		    	loadAlternativeText: function(viewport) {
		        	$('[data-websites-component="/components/textandimage/image"]').each(function(){
		    			if(viewport.is("xs") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-xs"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("sm") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-sm"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("md") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-md"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("lg") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-lg"));
		            	}
		        	});
		    	}
			};
	
			$(document).ready(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
			});

            Websites.Events.onBreakpointChanged(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
            });
		</script>
</div>

<script type="text/javascript">
		
			var Websites = Websites || {};
			Websites.FragmentPicture = Websites.FragmentPicture || {
				init: function(viewport) {
					Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(viewport);
				},
	
		    	loadAlternativeText: function(viewport) {
		        	$('[data-websites-component="/components/textandimage/image"]').each(function(){
		    			if(viewport.is("xs") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-xs"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("sm") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-sm"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("md") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-md"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("lg") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-lg"));
		            	}
		        	});
		    	}
			};
	
			$(document).ready(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
			});

            Websites.Events.onBreakpointChanged(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
            });
		</script>
</div>
</div>

<script>

        (function(){

        var dataLayerViewEventName = '' || '';
        var dataLayerViewLayerProperties = [];
        var $el;

        

        if(dataLayerViewEventName.trim().length) {

        var obj = {
        dataLayerViewEventName: dataLayerViewEventName,
        componentId: "c0f8a2f3-f931-47c7-b683-08fdcd7caabe_parsys_panelcontainer_76146_parsys_panelcontainer_copy__parsys_columns_1683152952_parsys3_panelcontainer_copy_parsys_textandimage" ,
        dataLayerViewLayerProperties: dataLayerViewLayerProperties
        };

        // IE11 trick (because IE11 don't know document.currentScript):
        https://stackoverflow.com/questions/403967/how-may-i-reference-the-script-tag-that-loaded-the-currently-executing-script
        if(document.currentScript){
        $el = document.currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        } else {
        var scripts = document.getElementsByTagName( 'script' );
        var currentScript = scripts[scripts.length - 1];
        $el = currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        }

        $el.setAttribute('data-dataLayerViewEventJson', JSON.stringify(
        Websites.DataLayer.cleanViewEventJSON(obj)));
        $el.setAttribute("data-dataLayerViewEvent", 'true');

        Websites.DataLayer.updateDataLayerViewEventElementsArray();

        }

        })();

        </script>
</div>
<script>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*
		*/

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

		</script></div>
</div>
</div>

			var Websites = Websites || {};
			Websites.FragmentPicture = Websites.FragmentPicture || {
				init: function(viewport) {
					Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(viewport);
				},
	
		    	loadAlternativeText: function(viewport) {
		        	$('[data-websites-component="/components/textandimage/image"]').each(function(){
		    			if(viewport.is("xs") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-xs"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("sm") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-sm"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("md") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-md"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("lg") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-lg"));
		            	}
		        	});
		    	}
			};
	
			$(document).ready(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
			});

            Websites.Events.onBreakpointChanged(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
            });
		</script>

<script>

        (function(){

        var dataLayerViewEventName = '' || '';
        var dataLayerViewLayerProperties = [];
        var $el;

        

        if(dataLayerViewEventName.trim().length) {

        var obj = {
        dataLayerViewEventName: dataLayerViewEventName,
        componentId: "c0f8a2f3-f931-47c7-b683-08fdcd7caabe_parsys_panelcontainer_76146_parsys_panelcontainer_copy__parsys_columns_1683152952_parsys6_panelcontainer_copy__parsys_textandimage" ,
        dataLayerViewLayerProperties: dataLayerViewLayerProperties
        };

        // IE11 trick (because IE11 don't know document.currentScript):
        https://stackoverflow.com/questions/403967/how-may-i-reference-the-script-tag-that-loaded-the-currently-executing-script
        if(document.currentScript){
        $el = document.currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        } else {
        var scripts = document.getElementsByTagName( 'script' );
        var currentScript = scripts[scripts.length - 1];
        $el = currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        }

        $el.setAttribute('data-dataLayerViewEventJson', JSON.stringify(
        Websites.DataLayer.cleanViewEventJSON(obj)));
        $el.setAttribute("data-dataLayerViewEvent", 'true');

        Websites.DataLayer.updateDataLayerViewEventElementsArray();

        }

        })();

        </script>

<script>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*
		*/

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

		</script></div>
</div>

<script type="text/javascript">
		
			var Websites = Websites || {};
			Websites.FragmentPicture = Websites.FragmentPicture || {
				init: function(viewport) {
					Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(viewport);
				},
	
		    	loadAlternativeText: function(viewport) {
		        	$('[data-websites-component="/components/textandimage/image"]').each(function(){
		    			if(viewport.is("xs") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-xs"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("sm") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-sm"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("md") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-md"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("lg") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-lg"));
		            	}
		        	});
		    	}
			};
	
			$(document).ready(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
			});

            Websites.Events.onBreakpointChanged(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
            });
		</script>
</div>
<script>
                (function(){
                    var eventInfo = {'dtmTracking' : [''], 'eventName' : '', 'elements' : [] };
                    
                    Websites.DataLayer.setLinkPayload(JSON.stringify(eventInfo));
                })();
			</script>
</a>
</div>
<div class="col-xs-12 text-image-text-container" data-text-image-text-container-style-lg="{'padding-top': '0px'}" data-text-image-text-container-style-md="{'padding-top': '0px'}" data-text-image-text-container-style-sm="{'padding-top': '0px'}" data-text-image-text-container-style-xs="{'padding-top': '0px'}" data-websites-component="/components/textandimage/text"></div>
</div>
<script>

        (function(){

        var dataLayerViewEventName = '' || '';
        var dataLayerViewLayerProperties = [];
        var $el;

        

        if(dataLayerViewEventName.trim().length) {

        var obj = {
        dataLayerViewEventName: dataLayerViewEventName,
        componentId: "c0f8a2f3-f931-47c7-b683-08fdcd7caabe_parsys_panelcontainer_21205_parsys_panelcontainer_copy_parsys_columns_parsys2_panelcontainer_parsys_textandimage" ,
        dataLayerViewLayerProperties: dataLayerViewLayerProperties
        };

        // IE11 trick (because IE11 don't know document.currentScript):
        https://stackoverflow.com/questions/403967/how-may-i-reference-the-script-tag-that-loaded-the-currently-executing-script
        if(document.currentScript){
        $el = document.currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        } else {
        var scripts = document.getElementsByTagName( 'script' );
        var currentScript = scripts[scripts.length - 1];
        $el = currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        }

        $el.setAttribute('data-dataLayerViewEventJson', JSON.stringify(
        Websites.DataLayer.cleanViewEventJSON(obj)));
        $el.setAttribute("data-dataLayerViewEvent", 'true');

        Websites.DataLayer.updateDataLayerViewEventElementsArray();

        }

        })();

        </script>
</div>
<script>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*
		*/

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

		</script></div>
</div>
</div>

        new Websites.Sticky({

            breakpoint: {
                lg: {
                    to: ""
                },
                md: {
                    to: ""
                },
                sm: {
                    to: "",
                },
                xs: {
                    to: ""
                }
            }
        });
    }
</script>
</div>

<script type="text/javascript">
		
			var Websites = Websites || {};
			Websites.FragmentPicture = Websites.FragmentPicture || {
				init: function(viewport) {
					Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(viewport);
				},
	
		    	loadAlternativeText: function(viewport) {
		        	$('[data-websites-component="/components/textandimage/image"]').each(function(){
		    			if(viewport.is("xs") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-xs"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("sm") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-sm"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("md") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-md"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("lg") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-lg"));
		            	}
		        	});
		    	}
			};
	
			$(document).ready(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
			});

            Websites.Events.onBreakpointChanged(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
            });
		</script>
</div>
<script>
                (function(){
                    var eventInfo = {'dtmTracking' : [''], 'eventName' : '', 'elements' : [] };
                    
                    Websites.DataLayer.setLinkPayload(JSON.stringify(eventInfo));
                })();
			</script>
</a>
</div>
<div class="col-xs-12 text-image-text-container" data-text-image-text-container-style-lg="{'padding-top': '0px'}" data-text-image-text-container-style-md="{'padding-top': '0px'}" data-text-image-text-container-style-sm="{'padding-top': '0px'}" data-text-image-text-container-style-xs="{'padding-top': '0px'}" data-websites-component="/components/textandimage/text"></div>

<script>

        (function(){

        var dataLayerViewEventName = '' || '';
        var dataLayerViewLayerProperties = [];
        var $el;

        

        if(dataLayerViewEventName.trim().length) {

        var obj = {
        dataLayerViewEventName: dataLayerViewEventName,
        componentId: "c0f8a2f3-f931-47c7-b683-08fdcd7caabe_parsys_panelcontainer_21205_parsys_panelcontainer_copy_parsys_columns_683200345_parsys1_panelcontainer_parsys_textandimage" ,
        dataLayerViewLayerProperties: dataLayerViewLayerProperties
        };

        // IE11 trick (because IE11 don't know document.currentScript):
        https://stackoverflow.com/questions/403967/how-may-i-reference-the-script-tag-that-loaded-the-currently-executing-script
        if(document.currentScript){
        $el = document.currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        } else {
        var scripts = document.getElementsByTagName( 'script' );
        var currentScript = scripts[scripts.length - 1];
        $el = currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        }

        $el.setAttribute('data-dataLayerViewEventJson', JSON.stringify(
        Websites.DataLayer.cleanViewEventJSON(obj)));
        $el.setAttribute("data-dataLayerViewEvent", 'true');

        Websites.DataLayer.updateDataLayerViewEventElementsArray();

        }

        })();

        </script>
</div>
<script>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*
		*/

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

		</script></div>
</div>
</div>

            breakpoint: {
                lg: {
                    to: ""
                },
                md: {
                    to: ""
                },
                sm: {
                    to: "",
                },
                xs: {
                    to: ""
                }
            }
        });
    }
</script>

<script>

        (function(){

        var dataLayerViewEventName = '' || '';
        var dataLayerViewLayerProperties = [];
        var $el;

        

        if(dataLayerViewEventName.trim().length) {

        var obj = {
        dataLayerViewEventName: dataLayerViewEventName,
        componentId: "c0f8a2f3-f931-47c7-b683-08fdcd7caabe_parsys_panelcontainer_76146_1652114589_parsys_panelcontainer_1720042281_parsys_textandimage_8290184" ,
        dataLayerViewLayerProperties: dataLayerViewLayerProperties
        };

        // IE11 trick (because IE11 don't know document.currentScript):
        https://stackoverflow.com/questions/403967/how-may-i-reference-the-script-tag-that-loaded-the-currently-executing-script
        if(document.currentScript){
        $el = document.currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        } else {
        var scripts = document.getElementsByTagName( 'script' );
        var currentScript = scripts[scripts.length - 1];
        $el = currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        }

        $el.setAttribute('data-dataLayerViewEventJson', JSON.stringify(
        Websites.DataLayer.cleanViewEventJSON(obj)));
        $el.setAttribute("data-dataLayerViewEvent", 'true');

        Websites.DataLayer.updateDataLayerViewEventElementsArray();

        }

        })();

        </script>
</div>
<script>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*
		*/

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

		</script></div>

<script type="text/javascript">
		
			var Websites = Websites || {};
			Websites.FragmentPicture = Websites.FragmentPicture || {
				init: function(viewport) {
					Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(viewport);
				},
	
		    	loadAlternativeText: function(viewport) {
		        	$('[data-websites-component="/components/textandimage/image"]').each(function(){
		    			if(viewport.is("xs") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-xs"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("sm") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-sm"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("md") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-md"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("lg") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-lg"));
		            	}
		        	});
		    	}
			};
	
			$(document).ready(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
			});

            Websites.Events.onBreakpointChanged(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
            });
		</script>

				},
	
		    	loadAlternativeText: function(viewport) {
		        	$('[data-websites-component="/components/textandimage/image"]').each(function(){
		    			if(viewport.is("xs") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-xs"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("sm") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-sm"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("md") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-md"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("lg") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-lg"));
		            	}
		        	});
		    	}
			};
	
			$(document).ready(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
			});

            Websites.Events.onBreakpointChanged(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);

        if(document.currentScript){
        $el = document.currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];

<script>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*
		*/

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

		</script></div>
</div>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*
		*/

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

        if(dataLayerViewEventName.trim().length) {

        var obj = {
        dataLayerViewEventName: dataLayerViewEventName,
        componentId: "c0f8a2f3-f931-47c7-b683-08fdcd7caabe_parsys_panelcontainer_91808_parsys_panelcontainer_1129347312_parsys_columns_copy_parsys2_panelcontainer_copy_parsys_panelcontainer_parsys_columns_copy_parsys2_textandimage" ,
        dataLayerViewLayerProperties: dataLayerViewLayerProperties
        };

        // IE11 trick (because IE11 don't know document.currentScript):
        https://stackoverflow.com/questions/403967/how-may-i-reference-the-script-tag-that-loaded-the-currently-executing-script
        if(document.currentScript){
        $el = document.currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        } else {
        var scripts = document.getElementsByTagName( 'script' );
        var currentScript = scripts[scripts.length - 1];
        $el = currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        }

        $el.setAttribute('data-dataLayerViewEventJson', JSON.stringify(
        Websites.DataLayer.cleanViewEventJSON(obj)));
        $el.setAttribute("data-dataLayerViewEvent", 'true');

        Websites.DataLayer.updateDataLayerViewEventElementsArray();

        }

        })();

        </script>

<script>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*
		*/

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

		</script></div>

                    (function () {
                        var $el;

                        var listeners = [];
                        

                        // IE11 trick (because IE11 don't know document.currentScript): https://stackoverflow.com/questions/403967/how-may-i-reference-the-script-tag-that-loaded-the-currently-executing-script
                        if (document.currentScript) {
                            $el = document.currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('a')[0];
                        } else {
                            var scripts = document.getElementsByTagName('script');
                            var currentScript = scripts[scripts.length - 1];
                            $el = currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByTagName('a')[0];
                        }

                        Websites.Product.Core.initContentQueue.push(function () {
                            Websites.Product.ButtonLink.initButtonLink({
                                $el: $el,
                                capsuleAlias: "",
                                listeners: listeners,
                                products: Websites.Product.Core.determineProductsArray("")
                            });
                        });
                    })();

			var Websites = Websites || {};
			Websites.FragmentPicture = Websites.FragmentPicture || {
				init: function(viewport) {
					Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(viewport);
				},
	
		    	loadAlternativeText: function(viewport) {
		        	$('[data-websites-component="/components/textandimage/image"]').each(function(){
		    			if(viewport.is("xs") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-xs"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("sm") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-sm"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("md") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-md"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("lg") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-lg"));
		            	}
		        	});
		    	}
			};
	
			$(document).ready(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
			});

            Websites.Events.onBreakpointChanged(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
            });
		</script>

<script>

        (function(){

        var dataLayerViewEventName = '' || '';
        var dataLayerViewLayerProperties = [];
        var $el;

        

        if(dataLayerViewEventName.trim().length) {

        var obj = {
        dataLayerViewEventName: dataLayerViewEventName,
        componentId: "c0f8a2f3-f931-47c7-b683-08fdcd7caabe_parsys_panelcontainer_91808_parsys_panelcontainer_1129347312_parsys_panelcontainer_11790_parsys_columns_copy_parsys2_panelcontainer_277102330_parsys_panelcontainer_parsys_textandimage" ,
        dataLayerViewLayerProperties: dataLayerViewLayerProperties
        };

        // IE11 trick (because IE11 don't know document.currentScript):
        https://stackoverflow.com/questions/403967/how-may-i-reference-the-script-tag-that-loaded-the-currently-executing-script
        if(document.currentScript){
        $el = document.currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        } else {
        var scripts = document.getElementsByTagName( 'script' );
        var currentScript = scripts[scripts.length - 1];
        $el = currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        }

        $el.setAttribute('data-dataLayerViewEventJson', JSON.stringify(
        Websites.DataLayer.cleanViewEventJSON(obj)));
        $el.setAttribute("data-dataLayerViewEvent", 'true');

        Websites.DataLayer.updateDataLayerViewEventElementsArray();

        }

        })();

        </script>

<script>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*
		*/

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

		</script></div>
</div>
</div>

			var Websites = Websites || {};
			Websites.FragmentPicture = Websites.FragmentPicture || {
				init: function(viewport) {
					Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(viewport);
				},
	
		    	loadAlternativeText: function(viewport) {
		        	$('[data-websites-component="/components/textandimage/image"]').each(function(){
		    			if(viewport.is("xs") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-xs"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("sm") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-sm"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("md") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-md"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("lg") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-lg"));
		            	}
		        	});
		    	}
			};
	
			$(document).ready(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
			});

            Websites.Events.onBreakpointChanged(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
            });
		</script>

<script>

        (function(){

        var dataLayerViewEventName = '' || '';
        var dataLayerViewLayerProperties = [];
        var $el;

        

        if(dataLayerViewEventName.trim().length) {

        var obj = {
        dataLayerViewEventName: dataLayerViewEventName,
        componentId: "c0f8a2f3-f931-47c7-b683-08fdcd7caabe_parsys_panelcontainer_91808_parsys_panelcontainer_1129347312_parsys_panelcontainer_11790_parsys_columns_copy_parsys3_panelcontainer_copy_parsys_panelcontainer_parsys_textandimage" ,
        dataLayerViewLayerProperties: dataLayerViewLayerProperties
        };

        // IE11 trick (because IE11 don't know document.currentScript):
        https://stackoverflow.com/questions/403967/how-may-i-reference-the-script-tag-that-loaded-the-currently-executing-script
        if(document.currentScript){
        $el = document.currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        } else {
        var scripts = document.getElementsByTagName( 'script' );
        var currentScript = scripts[scripts.length - 1];
        $el = currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        }

        $el.setAttribute('data-dataLayerViewEventJson', JSON.stringify(
        Websites.DataLayer.cleanViewEventJSON(obj)));
        $el.setAttribute("data-dataLayerViewEvent", 'true');

        Websites.DataLayer.updateDataLayerViewEventElementsArray();

        }

        })();

        </script>

<script>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*
		*/

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

		</script></div>
</div>
</div>

        dataLayerViewEventName: dataLayerViewEventName,
        componentId: "c0f8a2f3-f931-47c7-b683-08fdcd7caabe_parsys_panelcontainer_40138_parsys_panelcontainer_parsys_panelcontainer_parsys_columns_parsys2_panelcontainer_parsys_columns_parsys1_textandimage" ,
        dataLayerViewLayerProperties: dataLayerViewLayerProperties
        };

        // IE11 trick (because IE11 don't know document.currentScript):
        https://stackoverflow.com/questions/403967/how-may-i-reference-the-script-tag-that-loaded-the-currently-executing-script
        if(document.currentScript){
        $el = document.currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        } else {
        var scripts = document.getElementsByTagName( 'script' );
        var currentScript = scripts[scripts.length - 1];
        $el = currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        }

        $el.setAttribute('data-dataLayerViewEventJson', JSON.stringify(
        Websites.DataLayer.cleanViewEventJSON(obj)));
        $el.setAttribute("data-dataLayerViewEvent", 'true');

        Websites.DataLayer.updateDataLayerViewEventElementsArray();

        }

        })();

        </script>
</div>
<script>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*
		*/

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

		</script></div>
</div>

		    			} else if(viewport.is("lg") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-lg"));
		            	}
		        	});
		    	}

<script>

        (function(){

        var dataLayerViewEventName = '' || '';
        var dataLayerViewLayerProperties = [];
        var $el;

        

        if(dataLayerViewEventName.trim().length) {

        var obj = {
        dataLayerViewEventName: dataLayerViewEventName,
        componentId: "84f74d82-fc5c-4e9f-927c-b12d5eb18d43_parsys_panelcontainer_parsys_textandimage_434650514" ,
        dataLayerViewLayerProperties: dataLayerViewLayerProperties
        };

        // IE11 trick (because IE11 don't know document.currentScript):
        https://stackoverflow.com/questions/403967/how-may-i-reference-the-script-tag-that-loaded-the-currently-executing-script
        if(document.currentScript){
        $el = document.currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        } else {
        var scripts = document.getElementsByTagName( 'script' );
        var currentScript = scripts[scripts.length - 1];
        $el = currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        }

        $el.setAttribute('data-dataLayerViewEventJson', JSON.stringify(
        Websites.DataLayer.cleanViewEventJSON(obj)));
        $el.setAttribute("data-dataLayerViewEvent", 'true');

        Websites.DataLayer.updateDataLayerViewEventElementsArray();

        }

        })();

        </script>
</div>
<script>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*
		*/

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

		</script></div>
</div>
</div>

<script>

        (function(){

        var dataLayerViewEventName = '' || '';
        var dataLayerViewLayerProperties = [];
        var $el;

        

        if(dataLayerViewEventName.trim().length) {

        var obj = {
        dataLayerViewEventName: dataLayerViewEventName,
        componentId: "2ee536d5-5caf-4291-a925-9b39b05098b8_ws_layout_footer_footer_panelcontainer_parsys_panelcontainer_parsys_columns_1146045113_parsys2_columns_parsys1_textandimage" ,
        dataLayerViewLayerProperties: dataLayerViewLayerProperties
        };

        // IE11 trick (because IE11 don't know document.currentScript):
        https://stackoverflow.com/questions/403967/how-may-i-reference-the-script-tag-that-loaded-the-currently-executing-script
        if(document.currentScript){
        $el = document.currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        } else {
        var scripts = document.getElementsByTagName( 'script' );
        var currentScript = scripts[scripts.length - 1];
        $el = currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        }

        $el.setAttribute('data-dataLayerViewEventJson', JSON.stringify(
        Websites.DataLayer.cleanViewEventJSON(obj)));
        $el.setAttribute("data-dataLayerViewEvent", 'true');

        Websites.DataLayer.updateDataLayerViewEventElementsArray();

        }

        })();

        </script>
</div>
<script>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*
		*/

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

		</script>
</div>

<script type="text/javascript">
		
			var Websites = Websites || {};
			Websites.FragmentPicture = Websites.FragmentPicture || {
				init: function(viewport) {
					Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(viewport);
				},
	
		    	loadAlternativeText: function(viewport) {
		        	$('[data-websites-component="/components/textandimage/image"]').each(function(){
		    			if(viewport.is("xs") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-xs"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("sm") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-sm"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("md") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-md"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("lg") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-lg"));
		            	}
		        	});
		    	}
			};
	
			$(document).ready(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
			});

            Websites.Events.onBreakpointChanged(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
            });
		</script>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

        (function(){

        var dataLayerViewEventName = '' || '';
        var dataLayerViewLayerProperties = [];
        var $el;

        

        if(dataLayerViewEventName.trim().length) {

        var obj = {
        dataLayerViewEventName: dataLayerViewEventName,
        componentId: "2ee536d5-5caf-4291-a925-9b39b05098b8_ws_layout_footer_footer_panelcontainer_1411666172_parsys_collapse_1350503036_collapse_parsys_collapse_textandimage" ,
        dataLayerViewLayerProperties: dataLayerViewLayerProperties
        };

        // IE11 trick (because IE11 don't know document.currentScript):
        https://stackoverflow.com/questions/403967/how-may-i-reference-the-script-tag-that-loaded-the-currently-executing-script
        if(document.currentScript){
        $el = document.currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        } else {
        var scripts = document.getElementsByTagName( 'script' );
        var currentScript = scripts[scripts.length - 1];
        $el = currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        }

        $el.setAttribute('data-dataLayerViewEventJson', JSON.stringify(
        Websites.DataLayer.cleanViewEventJSON(obj)));
        $el.setAttribute("data-dataLayerViewEvent", 'true');

        Websites.DataLayer.updateDataLayerViewEventElementsArray();

        }

        })();

        </script>

<script>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*
		*/

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

		</script>
</div>
</div>

<script type="text/javascript">
		
			var Websites = Websites || {};
			Websites.FragmentPicture = Websites.FragmentPicture || {
				init: function(viewport) {
					Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(viewport);
				},
	
		    	loadAlternativeText: function(viewport) {
		        	$('[data-websites-component="/components/textandimage/image"]').each(function(){
		    			if(viewport.is("xs") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-xs"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("sm") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-sm"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("md") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-md"));
		    			} else if(viewport.is("lg") ) {
		    				$(this).attr("alt", $(this).data("picture-alttext-lg"));
		            	}
		        	});
		    	}
			};
	
			$(document).ready(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
			});

            Websites.Events.onBreakpointChanged(function(){
                Websites.FragmentPicture.loadAlternativeText(ResponsiveBootstrapToolkit);
            });
		</script>

        $el = currentScript.parentNode.getElementsByClassName('text-image-text-container')[0];
        }

        $el.setAttribute('data-dataLayerViewEventJson', JSON.stringify(
        Websites.DataLayer.cleanViewEventJSON(obj)));
        $el.setAttribute("data-dataLayerViewEvent", 'true');

        Websites.DataLayer.updateDataLayerViewEventElementsArray();

        }

        })();

        </script>
</div>
<script>

		/**
		* clickEventDownloadHandler()
		* Is used to handle download image action selected as an opening mode
		*
		*/

		var firstDownload = true;

		function clickEventDownloadHandler() {

		var link = this;
		var filename = link.dataset.linkpath;
		var newFile = filename.slice((filename.lastIndexOf(".") - 1 >>> 0) + 2);
		var fn = filename.substring(filename.lastIndexOf('/')+1);

		if (newFile) {

		if (firstDownload) {
		firstDownload = false;
		this.href = link.href.slice(0, link.href.lastIndexOf('.'));
		} else {
		this.href = link.href;
		}

		this.download = fn;

		} else {
		this.download = fn + ".html";
		}
		}

		</script>
</div>
